Rolling Stone termed as an inescapable &quot;multimedia bonanza&quot;.[549][550] Easter eggs and cryptic teasers became a common practice in contemporary pop music because of Swift.[551] Publications describe her discography as a music &quot;universe&quot; subject to analyses by fans, critics and journalists.[552][553][554] Swift maintains an active presence on social media and a close relationship with fans, to which many journalists attribute her success.[555][487][556] Her in-house management team is called 13 Management.[557]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC203" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="203" style="position:relative">Swift has endorsed many brands and businesses, having launched clothing lines with L.E.I. and Stella McCartney,[558][559] designed American Greetings cards and Jakks Pacific dolls,[560][561] released a number of fragrances with Elizabeth Arden,[562] and signed multi-year deals with AT&amp;T and Capital One.[563][564] She was a spokesperson for the National Hockey League&#039;s Nashville Predators and Sony Cyber-shot digital cameras,[565][566] and became the global ambassador for New York City in 2014 and Record Store Day in 2022.[567][568]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC204" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="204" style="position:relative">Social activism</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC205" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="205" style="position:relative">Further information: Political impact of Taylor Swift</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC206" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="206" style="position:relative">Swift identifies as a pro-choice feminist,[569] and is a founding signatory of the Time&#039;s Up movement against sexual harassment.[570] Specifically, she criticized the US Supreme Court&#039;s decision to end federal abortion rights in 2022.[571] Swift also advocates for LGBT rights,[572] and has called for the passing of the Equality Act, which prohibits discrimination based on sex, sexual orientation, and gender identity.[573][574] She performed during WorldPride NYC 2019 at the Stonewall Inn, a gay rights monument, and has donated to the LGBT organizations Tennessee Equality Project and GLAAD.[575][576][577]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC207" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="207" style="position:relative">A supporter of the March for Our Lives movement and gun control reform in the US,[578] Swift is a vocal critic of white supremacy, racism, and police brutality.[579][569] Following the George Floyd protests, she donated to the NAACP Legal Defense and Educational Fund and the Black Lives Matter movement,[580] called for the removal of Confederate monuments in Tennessee,[581] and advocated for Juneteenth to become a national holiday.[582] In 2020, Swift urged her fans to check their voter registration ahead of elections, which resulted in 65,000 people registering to vote within one day of her post,[583] and endorsed Joe Biden and Kamala Harris in the US presidential election.[584] She has openly criticized former president Donald Trump.[585]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC208" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="208" style="position:relative">Wealth</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC209" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="209" style="position:relative">Swift&#039;s net worth is estimated by Forbes and Bloomberg News at $1.1 billion as of October 2023, making her the first musician to achieve billionaire status &quot;solely based on her songs and performances&quot;.[586][587] Forbes named her the annual top-earning female musician in 2016, 2019, 2021, and 2022.[588] She was the highest-paid celebrity of 2016 with $170 million—a feat recognized by the Guinness World Records as the highest annual earnings ever for a female musician,[589] which she herself surpassed with $185 million in 2019.[590] Overall, Forbes listed Swift as the highest-paid female artist of the 2010s, earning $825 million.[591] She has also developed a real estate portfolio worth $150 million as of 2023, with properties in Nashville; Tribeca, Manhattan; Los Angeles (Samuel Goldwyn Estate); and Rhode Island (High Watch).[592]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC210" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="210" style="position:relative">Philanthropy</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC211" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="211" style="position:relative">Swift is known for her philanthropic efforts.[593] She ranked first on DoSomething&#039;s 2015 &quot;Gone Good&quot; list,[594] having received the Star of Compassion from the Tennessee Disaster Services and the Big Help Award from the Nickelodeon Kids&#039; Choice Awards for her &quot;dedication to helping others&quot; and &quot;inspiring others through action&quot;.[595][596] She donated $100,000 to the Red Cross to help the victims of the Iowa flood of 2008.[597] In 2009, she sang at BBC&#039;s Children in Need concert and raised £13,000 for the cause.[598] Swift has performed at charity relief events, including Sydney&#039;s Sound Relief concert.[599] In response to the May 2010 Tennessee floods, Swift donated $500,000.[600] In 2011, Swift used a dress rehearsal of her Speak Now tour as a benefit concert for victims of recent tornadoes in the US, raising more than $750,000.[601] In 2016, she donated $1 million to Louisiana flood relief efforts and $100,000 to the Dolly Parton Fire Fund.[602][603] Swift donated to food banks after Hurricane Harvey struck Houston in 2017 and at every stop of the Eras Tour in 2023;[604][605] she also directly employed local businesses throughout the tour and gave $55 million in bonus payments to her entire crew.[606][607] Swift donated $1 million for Tennessee tornado relief in 2020 and again in 2023.[608][609]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC212" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="212" style="position:relative">She is a supporter of the arts. A benefactor of the Nashville Songwriters Hall of Fame,[610] Swift has donated $75,000 to Nashville&#039;s Hendersonville High School to help refurbish the school auditorium,[611] $4 million to build a new education center at the Country Music Hall of Fame and Museum in Nashville,[612] $60,000 to the music departments of six US colleges,[613] and $100,000 to the Nashville Symphony.[614] Also a promoter of children&#039;s literacy, she has donated money and books to schools around the country.[615][616] In 2007, Swift partnered with the Tennessee Association of Chiefs of Police to launch a campaign to protect children from online predators.[617] She has donated items to several charities for auction, including the UNICEF Tap Project and MusiCares.[618] As recipient of the Academy of Country Music&#039;s Entertainer of the Year in 2011, Swift donated $25,000 to St. Jude Children&#039;s Research Hospital, Tennessee.[619] In 2012, Swift participated in the Stand Up to Cancer telethon, performing the charity single &quot;Ronan&quot;, which she wrote in memory of a four-year-old boy who died of neuroblastoma.[620] She has also donated $100,000 to the V Foundation for Cancer Research[621] and $50,000 to the Children&#039;s Hospital of Philadelphia.[622] Swift has encouraged young people to volunteer in their local communities as part of Global Youth Service Day.[623]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC213" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="213" style="position:relative">Swift donated to fellow singer-songwriter Kesha to help with her legal battles against Dr. Luke and to actress Mariska Hargitay&#039;s Joyful Heart Foundation.[593][624] During the COVID-19 pandemic, Swift donated to the World Health Organization and Feeding America,[625] and supported independent record stores.[626][627] Swift performed &quot;Soon You&#039;ll Get Better&quot; on the One World: Together At Home television special, a benefit concert curated by Lady Gaga for Global Citizen to raise funds for the World Health Organization&#039;s COVID-19 Solidarity Response Fund.[628] In 2018 and 2021, Swift donated to the Rape, Abuse &amp; Incest National Network in honor of Sexual Assault Awareness and Prevention Month.[593][629] She has made donations to her fans several times for their medical or academic expenses.[630] In December 2023, Swift attended Ramy Youssef&#039;s fundraiser for the Gaza Strip.[631]</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC214" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell"
